OBJECT Report 6086300 EM Status Report
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=EMW17.10.00.3.00.05;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Expense Management Statusbericht;
               ENU=Expense Management Status Report;
               NLD=Expense Management statusrapport];
    OnInitReport=VAR
                   EMSetup@1000 : Record 6086300;
                   Language@1001 : Record 8;
                 BEGIN
                   DateFilter := STRSUBSTNO('..%1',CALCDATE('<CM-1M+1D>',WORKDATE));

                   EMSetup.GET;
                   CurrReport.LANGUAGE := Language.GetLanguageID(EMSetup."Default Web/App Language");
                 END;

    OnPreReport=VAR
                  EMSetup@1000 : Record 6086300;
                  GLSetup@1001 : Record 98;
                BEGIN
                  EMSetup.GET;
                  GLSetup.GET;
                  DistanceUnit := FORMAT(EMSetup."Distance Unit");
                  LCYCode := GLSetup."LCY Code";
                END;

    PreviewMode=PrintLayout;
    UsageCategory=ReportsAndAnalysis;
  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 39  ;    ;DataItem;ContiniaUserSetup   ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086002;
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               UserResp@6086300 : Record 6086379;
                             BEGIN
                               IF UserResp.GetResponsibilityFilter <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                 ContiniaUserSetup.FILTERGROUP(2);
                                 ContiniaUserSetup.SETFILTER("Continia User ID",UserResp.GetResponsibilityFilter);
                                 ContiniaUserSetup.FILTERGROUP(0);
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  ContiniaUser.GET(ContiniaUserSetup."Continia User ID");
                                  IncludePosted := (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::All) OR (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::Posted);
                                  IncludeNotPosted := (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::All) OR (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::"Not Posted");;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 8   ;1   ;DataItem;Expenses            ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086320;
               DataItemTableView=;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SettlementNo <> '' THEN
                                 Expenses.SETFILTER("Settlement No.",SettlementNo);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ExpenseTmp@1000 : Record 6086320;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (NOT IncludePosted) AND Expenses.Posted THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (NOT IncludeNotPosted) AND (NOT Expenses.Posted) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF DateFilter <> '' THEN
                                    IF Expenses.Posted THEN BEGIN
                                      ExpenseTmp.RESET;
                                      ExpenseTmp.SETRANGE("Entry No.",Expenses."Entry No.");
                                      ExpenseTmp.SETFILTER("Document Date",DateFilter);
                                      IF ExpenseTmp.ISEMPTY THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    END;

                                  IF Expenses."No Refund" THEN BEGIN
                                    Expenses.Amount := -Expenses.Amount;
                                    Expenses."Amount (LCY)" := -Expenses."Amount (LCY)";
                                  END;

                                  IF Expenses."Settlement No." <> '' THEN
                                    SettlementExpense.GET(SettlementExpense."Document Type"::Settlement,Expenses."Settlement No.")
                                  ELSE
                                    CLEAR(SettlementExpense);

                                  AmtLCYForTotal := Expenses."Amount (LCY)";
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Continia User ID,Document Date;
               DataItemLink=Continia User ID=FIELD(Continia User ID) }

    { 64  ;2   ;Column  ;AllExpensesCaption  ;
               SourceExpr=AllExpensesLbl }

    { 3   ;2   ;Column  ;EntryNo_Expenses    ;
               SourceExpr=Expenses."Entry No." }

    { 6086300;2;Column  ;EntryNoCaption_Expenses;

    { 75  ;2   ;Column  ;AmountLCYForTotal_Expense;
               SourceExpr=AmtLCYForTotal }

    { 69  ;2   ;DataItem;ExpenseAllocation   ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086321;
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF ExpenseAllocation."No Refund" THEN BEGIN
                                    IF Expenses."Matched to Bank Transaction" THEN BEGIN
                                      AmtLCYForTotal := -ExpenseAllocation."Amount (LCY)";
                                      ExpenseAllocation.Amount := -ExpenseAllocation.Amount;
                                      ExpenseAllocation."Amount (LCY)" := -ExpenseAllocation."Amount (LCY)";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      AmtLCYForTotal := 0;
                                      ExpenseAllocation.Amount := 0;
                                      ExpenseAllocation."Amount (LCY)" := 0;
                                    END;
                                  END ELSE
                                    AmtLCYForTotal := ExpenseAllocation."Amount (LCY)";
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Expense Entry No.=FIELD(Entry No.) }

    { 68  ;3   ;Column  ;DescriptionCaption_ExpenseAllocation;
               SourceExpr=ExpenseAllocation.Description }

    { 1   ;1   ;DataItem;Mileage             ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086338;
               DataItemTableView=;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SettlementNo <> '' THEN
                                 Mileage.SETFILTER("Settlement No.",SettlementNo);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  MileageTmp@1000 : Record 6086338;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (NOT IncludePosted) AND Mileage.Posted THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (NOT IncludeNotPosted) AND (NOT Mileage.Posted) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF DateFilter <> '' THEN
                                    IF Mileage.Posted THEN BEGIN
                                      MileageTmp.RESET;
                                      MileageTmp.SETRANGE("Entry No.",Mileage."Entry No.");
                                      MileageTmp.SETFILTER("Registration Date",DateFilter);
                                      IF MileageTmp.ISEMPTY THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    END;

                                  IF Mileage."No Refund" THEN
                                    Mileage."Amount (LCY)" := -Mileage."Amount (LCY)";

                                  IF Mileage."Settlement No." <> '' THEN
                                    SettlementMileage.GET(SettlementMileage."Document Type"::Settlement,Mileage."Settlement No.")
                                  ELSE
                                    CLEAR(SettlementMileage);
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Continia User ID,Registration Date;
               DataItemLink=Continia User ID=FIELD(Continia User ID) }

    PROCEDURE SetGlobalVars@2(InclInReport@6086300 : 'All,Posted,Not Posted';DateFlt@1002 : Text[30]);
    BEGIN
      IncludeInReport := InclInReport;
      IncludePosted := (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::All) OR (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::Posted);
      IncludeNotPosted := (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::All) OR (IncludeInReport = IncludeInReport::"Not Posted");;
      DateFilter := DateFlt;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
